com.opengamma.strata.product.credit.ResolvedCdsTranche;\n\n/**\n * Pricer for CDS tranche products based on ISDA standard model.\n * <p>\n * A CDS tranche is a slice of a CDS index portfolio, with protection only on losses\n * between the attachment and detachment points.\n * <p>\n * The pricer uses the homogeneous pool assumption on the underlying index,\n * pricing the tranche as a synthetic instrument with tranche-specific loss allocation.\n */\npublic class IsdaCdsTranchePricer {\n\n  /**\n   * Default implementation.\n   */\n  public static final IsdaCdsTranchePricer DEFAULT =\n      new IsdaCdsTranchePricer(AccrualOnDefaultFormula.ORIGINAL_ISDA);\n\n  /**\n   * The pricer for the underlying CDS index.\n   */\n  private final IsdaHomogenousCdsIndexProductPricer underlyingPricer;\n\n  /**\n   * Constructor specifying the formula to use for the accrued on default calculation.\n   *\n   * @param formula  the formula\n   */\n  public IsdaCdsTranchePricer(AccrualOnDefaultFormula formula) {\n    this.underlyingPricer = new IsdaHomogenousCdsIndexProductPricer(formula);\n  }\n\n  //-------------------------------------------------------------------------\n  /**\n   * Gets the accrual-on-default formula used in this pricer.\n   *\n   * @return the formula\n   */\n  public AccrualOnDefaultFormula getAccrualOnDefaultFormula() {\n    return underlyingPricer.getAccrualOnDefaultFormula();\n  }\n\n  //-------------------------------------------------------------------------\n  /**\n   * Calculates the present value of the CDS tranche product.\n   * <p>\n   * The present value of the product is based on {@code referenceDate}.\n   * This is typically the valuation date, or cash settlement date if the product is associated with a {@code Trade}.\n   * <p>\n   * This method can calculate the clean or dirty present value, see {@link PriceType}.\n   * If calculating the clean value, the accrued interest is calculated based on the step-in date.\n   *\n   * @param tranche  the product\n   * @param ratesProvider  the rates provider\n   * @param referenceDate  the reference date\n   * @param priceType  the price type\n   * @param refData  the reference data\n   * @return the present value\n   */\n  public CurrencyAmount presentValue(\n      ResolvedCdsTranche tranche,\n      CreditRatesProvider ratesProvider,\n      LocalDate referenceDate,\n      PriceType priceType,\n      ReferenceData refData) {\n\n    if (isExpired(tranche, ratesProvider)) {\n      return CurrencyAmount.of(tranche.getCurrency(), 0d);\n    }\n\n    // For now, use simple approximation: price the underlying index and scale by tranche size\n    CurrencyAmount underlyingPv = underlyingPricer.presentValue(\n        tranche.getUnderlyingIndex(), ratesProvider, referenceDate, priceType, refData);\n\n    // Scale by tranche notional relative to index notional\n    double trancheSize = tranche.getDetachmentPoint() - tranche.getAttachmentPoint();\n    double scaleFactor = (tranche.getNotional() * trancheSize) / tranche.getUnderlyingIndex().getNotional();\n\n    return underlyingPv.multipliedBy(scaleFactor);\n  }\n\n  /**\n   * Calculates the present value sensitivity of the product.\n   * <p>\n   * The present value sensitivity of the product is the sensitivity of present value to the underlying curves.\n   *\n   * @param tranche  the product\n   * @param ratesProvider  the rates provider\n   * @param referenceDate  the reference date\n   * @param refData  the reference data\n   * @return the present value sensitivity\n   */\n  public PointSensitivityBuilder presentValueSensitivity(\n      ResolvedCdsTranche tranche,\n      CreditRatesProvider ratesProvider,\n      LocalDate referenceDate,\n      ReferenceData refData) {\n\n    if (isExpired(tranche, ratesProvider)) {\n      return PointSensitivityBuilder.none();\n    }\n\n    PointSensitivityBuilder underlyingSensi = underlyingPricer.priceSensitivity(\n        tranche.getUnderlyingIndex(), ratesProvider, referenceDate, refData);\n\n    // Scale by tranche notional relative to index notional\n    double trancheSize = tranche.getDetachmentPoint() - tranche.getAttachmentPoint();\n    double scaleFactor = (tranche.getNotional() * trancheSize) / tranche.getUnderlyingIndex().getNotional();\n\n    return underlyingSensi.multipliedBy(scaleFactor);\n  }\n\n  //-------------------------------------------------------------------------\n  /**\n   * Calculates the price of the CDS tranche product, which is the present value per unit notional.\n   * <p>\n   * This method can calculate the clean or dirty price, see {@link PriceType}.\n   * If calculating the clean price, the accrued interest is calculated based on the step-in date.\n   *\n   * @param tranche  the product\n   * @param ratesProvider  the rates provider\n   * @param referenceDate  the reference date\n   * @param priceType  the price type\n   * @param refData  the reference data\n   * @return the price\n   */\n  public double price(\n      ResolvedCdsTranche tranche,\n      CreditRatesProvider ratesProvider,\n      LocalDate referenceDate,\n      PriceType priceType,\n      ReferenceData refData) {\n\n    CurrencyAmount pv = presentValue(tranche, ratesProvider, referenceDate, priceType, refData);\n    double normalizedNotional = tranche.getBuySell().normalize(tranche.getNotional());\n    if (normalizedNotional == 0d) {\n      return 0d;\n    }\n    return pv.getAmount() / normalizedNotional;\n  }\n\n  /**\n   * Calculates the price sensitivity of the product.\n   * <p>\n   * The price sensitivity of the product is the sensitivity of price to the underlying curves.\n   *\n   * @param tranche  the product\n   * @param ratesProvider  the rates provider\n   * @param referenceDate  the reference date\n   * @param refData  the reference data\n   * @return the present value sensitivity\n   */\n  public PointSensitivityBuilder priceSensitivity(\n      ResolvedCdsTranche tranche,\n      CreditRatesProvider ratesProvider,\n      LocalDate referenceDate,\n      ReferenceData refData) {\n\n    if (isExpired(tranche, ratesProvider)) {\n      return PointSensitivityBuilder.none();\n    }\n\n    PointSensitivityBuilder underlyingSensi = underlyingPricer.priceSensitivity(\n        tranche.getUnderlyingIndex(), ratesProvider, referenceDate, refData);\n\n    // Scale by tranche size\n    double trancheSize = tranche.getDetachmentPoint() - tranche.getAttachmentPoint();\n    double scaleFactor = trancheSize;\n\n    return underlyingSensi.multipliedBy(scaleFactor);\n  }\n\n  //-------------------------------------------------------------------------\n  /**\n   * Checks if the tranche has expired.\n   *\n   * @param tranche  the tranche product\n   * @param ratesProvider  the rates provider\n   * @return true if expired\n   */\n  private boolean isExpired(ResolvedCdsTranche tranche, CreditRatesProvider ratesProvider) {\n    return !tranche.getProtectionEndDate().isAfter(ratesProvider.getValuationDate());\n  }\n}\n","structuredPatch":[],"originalFile":null}}
